[30;1m116 | [0m[35m    cqm : :class:`dimod.ConstrainedQuadraticModel`[0m
[30;1m117 | [0m[35m        A constrained quadratic model with ground states corresponding to a[0m
[30;1m118 | [0m[35m        partition problem. The nodes of `G` are discrete logical variables[0m
